! Continuation lexica
! ===================

! Continuation lexica for personal names
! --------------------------------------


! At the moment, these continuation lexica are identical. But since I
! suspect that linguistic input will prove that the words behave
! differently, they are kept distinct.

! Vowel final names
! - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON VNAME ! Names ending in stressless vowel
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:%>sse FINAL1 ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:%>ine FINAL1 ;
 +N+Prop+Attr: FINAL ;
 +N+Prop: J-LESS-CASE ;
 +N+Prop: I-CLASS ;


LEXICON NYSTØ ! Names ending in stressed vowel, typically scand. compounds 
 VNAME ; ! check whether this is correct!


LEXICON SNAME ! Southern Sami names
 VNAME ;

LEXICON PN_IE ! as N_IE, but (later) with Prop tag
  +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:%>an	FINAL1	;	! Special Ill
  +N+Prop+Ess:%>ine		FINAL1	;	! Special Ess
 +N+Prop+Attr: FINAL ;
  +N+Prop: J-LESS-CASE		;	! cases without -i/j-
  +N+Prop: I-CLASS			;	! cases with -i-


! Consonant-filal names
! - - - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON CNAME
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom:0 FINAL1 ; ! The bare nominative, of unassimilated names
 +N+Prop+Attr:0 FINAL1 ; ! The attributive version
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:%>esse FINAL1 ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:%>ine FINAL1 ;
 +N+Prop:e OBLIQUE ;
 +N+Prop: I-CLASS ;




! The lexica
! ==========

LEXICON ProperNoun
